Definition**\n```json\n{\n  "family": "shield-backend",\n  "networkMode": "awsvpc",\n  "requiresCompatibilities": ["FARGATE"],\n  "cpu": "1024",\n  "memory": "2048",\n  "containerDefinitions": [\n Database Connection Failed\n```bash\n# Check PostgreSQL is running\ndocker-compose ps postgres\n\n# Check logs\ndocker-compose logs postgres\n\n# Test connection\ndocker exec shield-postgres pg_isready -U shield_user\n```\n\n#### 2. Backend Not Starting\n```bash\n# Check logs\ndocker-compose logs backend\n\n# Verify environment variables\ndocker-compose exec backend env | grep DATABASE_URL\n\n# Restart service\ndocker-compose restart backend\n```\n\n#### 3. Frontend Build Errors\n```bash\n# Clear cache\ncd frontend\nrm -rf node_modules package-lock.json\nnpm install\n\n# Rebuild\nnpm run build\n```\n\n#### 4. Port Already in Use\n```bash\n# Find process using port\nlsof -i :8000  # Linux/Mac\nnetstat -ano | findstr :8000  # Windows\n\n# Kill process\nkill -9 <PID>  # Linux/Mac\ntaskkill /PID <PID> /F  # Windows\n```\n\n### Performance Optimization\n\n#### 1. Please install Docker first."\n        exit 1\n    fi\n    print_success "Docker is installed"\n    \n    # Check Docker Compose\n    if ! command -v docker-compose &> /dev/null; then\n        print_error "Docker Compose is not installed. Please install Docker Compose first."\n        exit 1\n    fi\n    print_success "Docker Compose is installed"\n    \n    # Check if Docker daemon is running\n    if ! docker info &> /dev/null; then\n        print_error "Docker daemon is not running. Please start Docker first."\n        exit 1\n    fi\n    print_success "Docker daemon is running"\n}\n\n# Check if services are already running\ncheck_running_services() {\n    print_info "Checking for running services..."\n    \n    if docker-compose ps | grep -q "Up"; then\n        print_warning "Some services are already running"\n        read -p "Do you want to restart them? (y/n) " -n 1 -r\n        echo\n        if [[ $REPLY =~ ^[Yy]$ ]]; then\n            print_info "Stopping existing services..."\n            docker-compose down\n        else\n            print_info "Keeping existing services running"\n            return 1\n        fi\n    fi\n    return 0\n}\n\n# Start services\nstart_services() {\n    print_info "Starting iTechSmart Shield services..."\n    \n    # Pull latest images\n    print_info "Pulling Docker images..."\n    docker-compose pull\n    \n    # Build images\n    print_info "Building Docker images..."\n    docker-compose build\n    \n    # Start services\n    print_info "Starting services..."\n    docker-compose up -d\n    \n    print_success "Services started successfully!"\n}\n\n# Wait for services to be healthy\nwait_for_services() {\n    print_info "Waiting for services to be ready..."\n    \n    # Wait for PostgreSQL\n    print_info "Waiting for PostgreSQL..."\n    timeout=60\n    counter=0\n    until docker-compose exec -T postgres pg_isready -U shield_user &> /dev/null; do\n        sleep 2\n        counter=$((counter + 2))\n        if [ $counter -ge $timeout ]; then\n            print_error "PostgreSQL failed to start within $timeout seconds"\n            exit 1\n        fi\n    done\n    print_success "PostgreSQL is ready"\n    \n    # Wait for Redis\n    print_info "Waiting for Redis..."\n    counter=0\n    until docker-compose exec -T redis redis-cli ping &> /dev/null; do\n        sleep 2\n        counter=$((counter + 2))\n        if [ $counter -ge $timeout ]; then\n            print_error "Redis failed to start within $timeout seconds"\n            exit 1\n        fi\n    done\n    print_success "Redis is ready"\n    \n    # Wait for Elasticsearch\n    print_info "Waiting for Elasticsearch..."\n    counter=0\n    until curl -s http://localhost:9200/_cluster/health &> /dev/null; do\n        sleep 2\n        counter=$((counter + 2))\n        if [ $counter -ge $timeout ]; then\n            print_error "Elasticsearch failed to start within $timeout seconds"\n            exit 1\n        fi\n    done\n    print_success "Elasticsearch is ready"\n    \n    # Wait for Backend\n    print_info "Waiting for Backend API..."\n    counter=0\n    until curl -s http://localhost:8000/health &> /dev/null; do\n        sleep 2\n        counter=$((counter + 2))\n        if [ $counter -ge $timeout ]; then\n            print_error "Backend API failed to start within $timeout seconds"\n            exit 1\n        fi\n    done\n    print_success "Backend API is ready"\n    \n    # Wait for Frontend\n    print_info "Waiting for Frontend..."\n    counter=0\n    until curl -s http://localhost:3000 &> /dev/null; do\n        sleep 2\n        counter=$((counter + 2))\n        if [ $counter -ge $timeout ]; then\n            print_error "Frontend failed to start within $timeout seconds"\n            exit 1\n        fi\n    done\n    print_success "Frontend is ready"\n}\n\n# Display service information\ndisplay_info() {\n    echo ""\n    print_success "iTechSmart Shield is now running!"\n    echo ""\n    echo -e "${GREEN}═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════${NC}"\n    echo -e "${GREEN}Access URLs:${NC}"\n    echo -e "  ${BLUE}Frontend:${NC}        http://localhost:3000"\n    echo -e "  ${BLUE}Backend API:${NC}     http://localhost:8000"\n    echo -e "  ${BLUE}API Docs:${NC}        http://localhost:8000/docs"\n    echo -e "  ${BLUE}PostgreSQL:${NC}      localhost:5432"\n    echo -e "  ${BLUE}Redis:${NC}           localhost:6379"\n    echo -e "  ${BLUE}Elasticsearch:${NC}   http://localhost:9200"\n    echo ""\n    echo -e "${GREEN}Default Credentials:${NC}"\n    echo -e "  ${BLUE}Database:${NC}        shield_user / shield_pass_2024"\n    echo ""\n    echo -e "${GREEN}Useful Commands:${NC}"\n    echo -e "  ${BLUE}View logs:${NC}       docker-compose logs -f"\n    echo -e "  ${BLUE}Stop services:${NC}   docker-compose down"\n    echo -e "  ${BLUE}Restart:${NC}         docker-compose restart"\n    echo -e "  ${BLUE}Status:${NC}          docker-compose ps"\n    echo -e "${GREEN}═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════${NC}"\n    echo ""\n}\n\n# Show logs\nshow_logs() {\n    print_info "Showing service logs (Ctrl+C to exit)..."\n    docker-compose logs -f\n}\n\n# Main execution\nmain() {\n    print_banner\n    \n    # Check prerequisites\n    check_prerequisites\n    \n    # Check running services\n    if ! check_running_services; then\n        display_info\n        read -p "Do you want to view logs? (y/n) " -n 1 -r\n        echo\n        if [[ $REPLY =~ ^[Yy]$ ]]; then\n            show_logs\n        fi\n        exit 0\n    fi\n    \n    # Start services\n    start_services\n    \n    # Wait for services\n    wait_for_services\n    \n    # Display information\n    display_info\n    \n    # Ask if user wants to see logs\n    read -p "Do you want to view logs? (y/n) " -n 1 -r\n    echo\n    if [[ $REPLY =~ ^[Yy]$ ]]; then\n        show_logs\n    fi\n}\n\n# Run main function\nmain\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

Create calculated fields and metrics\n- **Role-Based Access** - Granular permissions and data security\n- **API Access** - Programmatic access to analytics\n- **White-Label** - Customize branding and appearance\n\n## 🏗️ Architecture\n\n### Technology Stack\n\n**Backend:**\n- FastAPI (Python 3.11)\n- PostgreSQL 15 (Metadata & user data)\n- ClickHouse (Analytics database)\n- Redis (Caching & real-time data)\n- Celery (Background jobs)\n- Apache Superset (Embedded analytics)\n\n**Frontend:**\n- React 18 with TypeScript\n- D3.js (Advanced visualizations)\n- Chart.js (Standard charts)\n- Recharts (React charts)\n- AG Grid (Data tables)\n- Tailwind CSS\n- React Query (Data fetching)\n\n**Infrastructure:**\n- Docker & Docker Compose\n- Nginx (Reverse proxy)\n- MinIO (Object storage)\n- RabbitMQ (Message queue)\n\n## 🚀 Quick Start\n\n### Prerequisites\n- Docker 24.0+\n- Docker Compose 2.20+\n- Node.js 20+ (for local development)\n- Python 3.11+ (for local development)\n\n### Installation\n\n1. **Clone and navigate**\n```bash\ncd itechsmart-pulse\n```\n\n2. **Start services**\n```bash\ndocker-compose up -d\n```\n\n3. **Access the application**\n- Frontend: http://localhost:3000\n- Backend API: http://localhost:8000\n- API Documentation: http://localhost:8000/docs\n\n## 📊 Dashboard Types\n\n### Pre-built Dashboards\n1. **Executive Dashboard** -
